\doxysubsection{详细描述}
\subsubsection*{template$<$typename RCU, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, class Traits$>$\newline
class cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Lazy\+List$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}
Lazy ordered single-\/linked list (template specialization for \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1urcu_cds_urcu_desc}{RCU}) 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_LazyList_rcu}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_LazyList_rcu}%
 Usually, ordered single-\/linked list is used as a building block for the hash table implementation. The complexity of searching is {\ttfamily O(\+N)}.

Template arguments\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily RCU} -\/ one of \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1urcu_cds_urcu_gc}{RCU type}
\item {\ttfamily T} -\/ type to be stored in the list
\item {\ttfamily Traits} -\/ type traits. See {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1intrusive_1_1lazy__list_1_1traits}{lazy\+\_\+list\+::traits}} for explanation. It is possible to declare option-\/based list with {\ttfamily cds\+::intrusive\+::lazy\+\_\+list\+::make\+\_\+traits} metafunction instead of {\ttfamily Traits} template argument.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Usage}
Before including {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\doxylink{intrusive_2lazy__list__rcu_8h}{cds/intrusive/lazy\+\_\+list\+\_\+rcu.\+h}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} you should include appropriate RCU header file, see \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1urcu_cds_urcu_gc}{RCU type} for list of existing RCU class and corresponding header files. For example, for \doxylink{classcds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01general__buffered_3_01_buffer_00_01_lock_00_01_backoff_01_4_01_4_cds_urcu_general_buffered_gc}{general-\/purpose buffered RCU} you should include\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{preprocessor}{\#include\ <\mbox{\hyperlink{general__buffered_8h}{cds/urcu/general\_buffered.h}}>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{preprocessor}{\#include\ <\mbox{\hyperlink{intrusive_2lazy__list__rcu_8h}{cds/intrusive/lazy\_list\_rcu.h}}>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ Now,\ you\ can\ declare\ lazy\ list\ for\ type\ Foo\ and\ default\ traits:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{typedef}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{cds::intrusive::LazyList<cds::urcu::gc<\ cds::urcu::general\_buffered<>}}\ >,\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{Foo}}\ >\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{rcu\_lazy\_list}};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

Item counting policy used 

\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_af2519eda73d16ae0b6fba8c8dc89b303}\index{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!iterator@{iterator}}
\index{iterator@{iterator}!cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{iterator}{iterator}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_af2519eda73d16ae0b6fba8c8dc89b303} 
typedef iterator\+\_\+type$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a65e9886d74aaee76545e83dd09011727}{false}}$>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Lazy\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::iterator}



Forward iterator 

The forward iterator for lazy list has some features\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item it has no post-\/increment operator
\item to protect the value, the iterator contains a GC-\/specific guard + another guard is required locally for increment operator. For some GC ({\ttfamily \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1gc_af0523881f089593a7559d194ee2b5dd9}{gc\+::\+HP}}), a guard is limited resource per thread, so an exception (or assertion) "{}no free guard"{} may be thrown if a limit of guard count per thread is exceeded.
\item The iterator cannot be moved across thread boundary since it contains GC\textquotesingle{}s guard that is thread-\/private GC data.
\item Iterator ensures thread-\/safety even if you delete the item that iterator points to. However, in case of concurrent deleting operations it is no guarantee that you iterate all item in the list. Moreover, a crash is possible when you try to iterate the next element that has been deleted by concurrent thread.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
Use this iterator on the concurrent container for debugging purpose only. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

Forward iterator 

You may safely use iterators in multi-\/threaded environment only under RCU lock. Otherwise, a crash is possible if another thread deletes the item the iterator points to. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_acdedb60505bcd3506e49bd0e5e6ddcf9}\index{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!key\_comparator@{key\_comparator}}

\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a1793ba09820f165649e0353719ab755c}\index{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!clear@{clear}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a1793ba09820f165649e0353719ab755c} 
template$<$typename RCU, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, class Traits$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Lazy\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::clear (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Clears the list using default disposer 

The function clears the list using default (provided in class template) disposer functor.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. Note that depending on RCU type used the \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a0b763258177d3c090f135411d575c302}{disposer} call can be deferred.

The function can throw {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1urcu_1_1rcu__deadlock}{cds\+::urcu\+::rcu\+\_\+deadlock}} exception if deadlock is encountered and deadlock checking policy is {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1opt_1_1v_1_1rcu__throw__deadlock}{opt\+::v\+::rcu\+\_\+throw\+\_\+deadlock}}. 函数调用图\+:
% FIG 1

\index{contains@{contains}!cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Lazy\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::contains (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Checks whether the map contains {\ttfamily key} using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

The function is an analog of {\ttfamily contains( key )} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily Less} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the list. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a09aede3b00da7244a39b091ba2865be0}\index{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!contains@{contains}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_add3d42f975c4528d1d8b82a651bbe1f4} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Lazy\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::erase (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Func}]{func}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Deletes the item from the list 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_cds_intrusive_LazyList_hp_erase_func}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_cds_intrusive_LazyList_hp_erase_func}%
The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} in the list, call {\ttfamily func} functor with item found, unlinks it from the list, and returns {\ttfamily true}. The {\ttfamily Func} interface is 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{operator()}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{value\_type}}\ \textcolor{keyword}{const}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{item}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}


If {\ttfamily key} is not found the function return {\ttfamily false}.

{\ttfamily disposer} specified in {\ttfamily Traits} is called for deleted item. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_a7e5ad059410155179ce85be20085ddc3}\index{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!erase@{erase}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{erase()}{erase()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_a7e5ad059410155179ce85be20085ddc3}

Deletes the item from the list 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_cds_intrusive_LazyList_hp_erase_val}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_cds_intrusive_LazyList_hp_erase_val}%
The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} in the list, unlinks it from the list, and returns {\ttfamily true}. If the item with the key equal to {\ttfamily key} is not found the function return {\ttfamily false}.

{\ttfamily disposer} specified in {\ttfamily Traits} is called for deleted item. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a1c9d3a723d0447f0b78280c1040f456a}\index{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!erase@{erase}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a1c9d3a723d0447f0b78280c1040f456a}

\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Lazy\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::erase (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Deletes the item from the list 

The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} in the list, unlinks it from the list, and returns {\ttfamily true}. If the item with the key equal to {\ttfamily key} is not found the function return {\ttfamily false}.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. The RCU should not be locked. Note that depending on RCU type used the \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a0b763258177d3c090f135411d575c302}{disposer} call can be deferred.

{\ttfamily disposer} specified in {\ttfamily Traits} is called for deleted item.

The function can throw \doxylink{classcds_1_1urcu_1_1rcu__deadlock_cds_urcu_rcu_deadlock}{cds\+::urcu\+::rcu\+\_\+deadlock} exception if deadlock is encountered and deadlock checking policy is {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1opt_1_1v_1_1rcu__throw__deadlock}{opt\+::v\+::rcu\+\_\+throw\+\_\+deadlock}}. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_acef16b05243c6507db3156d52f36f03a}\index{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!erase@{erase}}
\index{erase@{erase}!cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{erase()}{erase()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [4/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_acef16b05243c6507db3156d52f36f03a} 
template$<$typename RCU, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, class Traits$>$ \\
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}}, typename Func$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Lazy\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::erase (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Func}]{func}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Deletes the item from the list 

The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} in the list, call {\ttfamily func} functor with item found, unlinks it from the list, and returns {\ttfamily true}. The {\ttfamily Func} interface is 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{operator()}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{value\_type}}\ \textcolor{keyword}{const}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{item}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}


If the item with the key equal to {\ttfamily key} is not found the function return {\ttfamily false}.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. The RCU should not be locked. Note that depending on RCU type used the \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a0b763258177d3c090f135411d575c302}{disposer} call can be deferred.

{\ttfamily disposer} specified in {\ttfamily Traits} is called for deleted item.

The function can throw \doxylink{classcds_1_1urcu_1_1rcu__deadlock_cds_urcu_rcu_deadlock}{cds\+::urcu\+::rcu\+\_\+deadlock} exception if deadlock is encountered and deadlock checking policy is {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1opt_1_1v_1_1rcu__throw__deadlock}{opt\+::v\+::rcu\+\_\+throw\+\_\+deadlock}}. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_acca4c64a076a29fac333fead8b6fb78c}\index{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!erase\_with@{erase\_with}}
\index{erase\_with@{erase\_with}!cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{erase\_with()}{erase\_with()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_acca4c64a076a29fac333fead8b6fb78c} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Lazy\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::erase\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{, }\item[{Func}]{func}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Deletes the item from the list using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_cds_intrusive_LazyList_hp_erase_func}{erase(Q const\&, Func)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the list.

{\ttfamily disposer} specified in {\ttfamily Traits} is called for deleted item. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_a2276e0cfa027b8bf6be8ac841d31b952}\index{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!erase\_with@{erase\_with}}

Deletes the item from the list using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

The function is an analog of {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_acef16b05243c6507db3156d52f36f03a}{erase(\+Q const\&, Func)}} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the list.

\index{extract@{extract}!cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{extract()}{extract()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_ac39cc38179cbb4a8f8f57e6be1797c45} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_a459f0916cee40b5ab5916d45b2daa2d4}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Lazy\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts the item from the list with specified {\ttfamily key} 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_cds_intrusive_LazyList_hp_extract}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_cds_intrusive_LazyList_hp_extract}%
The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily key}, unlinks it from the list, and returns it as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_a459f0916cee40b5ab5916d45b2daa2d4}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}}. If {\ttfamily key} is not found the function returns an empty guarded pointer.

Note the compare functor should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} that can be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_af8e0fb00fa1f61ebacadce944ed1e301}{value\+\_\+type}}.

The \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a0b763258177d3c090f135411d575c302}{disposer} specified in {\ttfamily Traits} class template parameter is called automatically by garbage collector {\ttfamily GC} specified in class\textquotesingle{} template parameters when returned {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_a459f0916cee40b5ab5916d45b2daa2d4}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object will be destroyed or released. \begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Each {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_a459f0916cee40b5ab5916d45b2daa2d4}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object uses the GC\textquotesingle{}s guard that can be limited resource.
\end{DoxyNote}

\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a332b4ef61325a6d0dffe1799c1503115}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Lazy\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts an item from the list 

The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} in the list, unlinks it from the list, and returns \doxylink{classcds_1_1urcu_1_1exempt__ptr}{exempt\+\_\+ptr} pointer to an item found. If the item is not found the function returns empty {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a332b4ef61325a6d0dffe1799c1503115}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}}.

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
The function does NOT call RCU read-\/side lock or synchronization, and does NOT dispose the item found. It just unlinks the item from the list and returns a pointer to it. You should manually lock RCU before calling this function, and you should manually release the returned exempt pointer outside the RCU lock region before reusing returned pointer.
\end{DoxyNote}

Extracts the item from the list with comparing functor {\ttfamily pred} 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_cds_intrusive_LazyList_hp_extract}{extract(Q const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} predicate is used for key comparing.

{\ttfamily Less} functor has the semantics like {\ttfamily std\+::less} but should take arguments of type \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_af8e0fb00fa1f61ebacadce944ed1e301}{value\+\_\+type} and {\ttfamily Q} in any order. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the list. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a86f59844d2e35a7b5630363a8188e1b9}\index{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!extract\_with@{extract\_with}}

Extracts an item from the list using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

This function is the analog for {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ab83445c19c01e993b8a24b52e2bdda6f}{extract(\+Q const\&)}}.

The {\ttfamily pred} is a predicate used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ae30429b4e19a540d98e4764b1ea45dd4}{key\+\_\+comparator}. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_a5cc9ac89103e64aae17e8247c379f666}\index{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!find@{find}}

Finds the key {\ttfamily key} 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_cds_intrusive_LazyList_hp_find}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_cds_intrusive_LazyList_hp_find}%
The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and calls the functor {\ttfamily f} for item found. The interface of {\ttfamily Func} functor is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{operator()}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{item}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{Q}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{key}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily item} is the item found, {\ttfamily key} is the {\ttfamily find} function argument.

The functor may change non-\/key fields of {\ttfamily item}. While the functor {\ttfamily f} is calling the item {\ttfamily item} is locked.

The function returns {\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily key} is found, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a49d1ef565ab23ed7e45b5f85016a410d}\index{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!find@{find}}

Finds {\ttfamily key} and return the item found 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_cds_intrusive_LazyList_hp_get}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_cds_intrusive_LazyList_hp_get}%
The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and returns an guarded pointer to it. If {\ttfamily key} is not found the function returns an empty guarded pointer.

The \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a0b763258177d3c090f135411d575c302}{disposer} specified in {\ttfamily Traits} class template parameter is called by garbage collector {\ttfamily GC} automatically when returned {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_a459f0916cee40b5ab5916d45b2daa2d4}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object will be destroyed or released. \begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Each {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_a459f0916cee40b5ab5916d45b2daa2d4}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object uses one GC\textquotesingle{}s guard which can be limited resource.
\end{DoxyNote}

Finds the key {\ttfamily key} and return the item found 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_LazyList_rcu_get}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_LazyList_rcu_get}%
The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and returns the pointer to item found. If {\ttfamily key} is not found it returns {\ttfamily nullptr}.

Note the compare functor should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} that can be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_af8e0fb00fa1f61ebacadce944ed1e301}{value\+\_\+type}}.

RCU should be locked before call of this function. Returned item is valid only while RCU is locked\+:

\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_a459f0916cee40b5ab5916d45b2daa2d4}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Lazy\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::get\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Finds {\ttfamily key} and return the item found 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_cds_intrusive_LazyList_hp_get}{get( Q const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for comparing the keys.

{\ttfamily Less} functor has the semantics like {\ttfamily std\+::less} but should take arguments of type \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_af8e0fb00fa1f61ebacadce944ed1e301}{value\+\_\+type} and {\ttfamily Q} in any order. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the list. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a5e3cfccef52cd969bf5212704aa8a7ad}\index{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!get\_with@{get\_with}}
\index{get\_with@{get\_with}!cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a5e3cfccef52cd969bf5212704aa8a7ad}

template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}}, typename Less$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_af8e0fb00fa1f61ebacadce944ed1e301}{value\+\_\+type}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Lazy\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::get\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Finds the key {\ttfamily key} and return the item found 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_LazyList_rcu_get}{get(Q const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for comparing the keys.

{\ttfamily Less} functor has the semantics like {\ttfamily std\+::less} but should take arguments of type \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_af8e0fb00fa1f61ebacadce944ed1e301}{value\+\_\+type} and {\ttfamily Q} in any order. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the list. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_adc05128f9b80c622f4faf7462906e40c}\index{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!insert@{insert}}

Inserts new node 

The function inserts {\ttfamily val} in the list if the list does not contain an item with key equal to {\ttfamily val}.

Returns {\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily val} is linked into the list, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a9f34638f3e41c0cf749c51c12537b134}\index{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!insert@{insert}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Lazy\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::insert (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_af8e0fb00fa1f61ebacadce944ed1e301}{value\+\_\+type}} \&}]{val}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Inserts new node 

The function inserts {\ttfamily val} in the list if the list does not contain an item with key equal to {\ttfamily val}.

Returns {\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily val} is linked into the list, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_adeea7e8b33b338329b2825ad6b12887f}\index{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!insert@{insert}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{insert()}{insert()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [3/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_adeea7e8b33b338329b2825ad6b12887f} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Lazy\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::insert (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_af8e0fb00fa1f61ebacadce944ed1e301}{value\+\_\+type}} \&}]{val}{, }\item[{Func}]{f}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Inserts new node 

This function is intended for derived non-\/intrusive containers.

The function allows to split new item creating into two part\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item create item with key only
\item insert new item into the list
\item if inserting is success, calls {\ttfamily f} functor to initialize value-\/field of {\ttfamily val}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor signature is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{benchmarks_2async__task_2async__task_8hpp_abce53bb5cc1ee70cdc013fd9b93547eb}{func}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_af8e0fb00fa1f61ebacadce944ed1e301}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{val}}\ );}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily val} is the item inserted. While the functor {\ttfamily f} is called the item {\ttfamily val} is locked so the functor has an exclusive access to the item. The user-\/defined functor is called only if the inserting is success. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a65b7940a8952fc14aabff5c92b584bec}\index{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!insert@{insert}}
\index{insert@{insert}!cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{insert()}{insert()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [4/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a65b7940a8952fc14aabff5c92b584bec} 
template$<$typename RCU, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, class Traits$>$ \\
template$<$typename Func$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Lazy\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::insert (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_af8e0fb00fa1f61ebacadce944ed1e301}{value\+\_\+type}} \&}]{val}{, }\item[{Func}]{f}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Inserts new node 

This function is intended for derived non-\/intrusive containers.

The function allows to split new item creating into two part\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item create item with key only
\item insert new item into the list
\item if inserting is success, calls {\ttfamily f} functor to initialize value-\/field of {\ttfamily val}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor signature is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{benchmarks_2async__task_2async__task_8hpp_abce53bb5cc1ee70cdc013fd9b93547eb}{func}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_af8e0fb00fa1f61ebacadce944ed1e301}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{val}}\ );}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily val} is the item inserted. While the functor {\ttfamily f} is working the item {\ttfamily val} is locked. The user-\/defined functor is called only if the inserting is success. 函数调用图\+:

size\+\_\+t \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Lazy\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_ac42c05b5701aef6bab82675cf3b55fee}{\+::size}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Returns list\textquotesingle{}s item count 

The value returned depends on item counter provided by {\ttfamily Traits}. For {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1atomicity_1_1empty__item__counter}{atomicity\+::empty\+\_\+item\+\_\+counter}}, this function always returns 0.

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Even if you use real item counter and it returns 0, this fact does not mean that the list is empty. To check list emptiness use {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_adb7cbb7bc3b3bae117f6242b242d2de7}{empty()}} method. 
\end{DoxyNote}

Returns list\textquotesingle{}s item count

\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Lazy\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::unlink (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_af8e0fb00fa1f61ebacadce944ed1e301}{value\+\_\+type}} \&}]{val}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Unlinks the item {\ttfamily val} from the list 

The function searches the item {\ttfamily val} in the list and unlink it from the list if it is found and it is equal to {\ttfamily val}.

Difference between \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a1c9d3a723d0447f0b78280c1040f456a}{erase} and {\ttfamily unlink} functions\+: {\ttfamily erase} finds {\itshape a key} and deletes the item found. {\ttfamily unlink} finds an item by key and deletes it only if {\ttfamily val} is an item of that list, i.\+e. the pointer to item found is equal to {\ttfamily  \&val }.

The function returns {\ttfamily true} if success and {\ttfamily false} otherwise.

{\ttfamily disposer} specified in {\ttfamily Traits} is called for unlinked item. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a4565d8f627a76d3717966ea069779adb}\index{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!unlink@{unlink}}
\index{unlink@{unlink}!cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{unlink()}{unlink()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a4565d8f627a76d3717966ea069779adb} 
template$<$typename RCU, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, class Traits$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Lazy\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::unlink (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_af8e0fb00fa1f61ebacadce944ed1e301}{value\+\_\+type}} \&}]{val}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Unlinks the item {\ttfamily val} from the list 

The function searches the item {\ttfamily val} in the list and unlink it from the list if it is found and it is equal to {\ttfamily val}.

Difference between {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a1c9d3a723d0447f0b78280c1040f456a}{erase()}} and {\ttfamily unlink}() functions\+: {\ttfamily erase}() finds {\itshape a key} and deletes the item found. {\ttfamily unlink}() finds an item by key and deletes it only if {\ttfamily val} is an item of that list, i.\+e. the pointer to item found is equal to {\ttfamily  \&val }.

The function returns {\ttfamily true} if success and {\ttfamily false} otherwise.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. The RCU should not be locked. Note that depending on RCU type used the \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a0b763258177d3c090f135411d575c302}{disposer} call can be deferred.

{\ttfamily disposer} specified in {\ttfamily Traits} is called for unlinked item.

The function can throw {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1urcu_1_1rcu__deadlock}{cds\+::urcu\+::rcu\+\_\+deadlock}} exception if deadlock is encountered and deadlock checking policy is {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1opt_1_1v_1_1rcu__throw__deadlock}{opt\+::v\+::rcu\+\_\+throw\+\_\+deadlock}}. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_a9b839c811a4692664f3b616b7a0332d6}\index{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!update@{update}}
\index{update@{update}!cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{update()}{update()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_a9b839c811a4692664f3b616b7a0332d6} 
std\+::pair$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Lazy\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_af8e0fb00fa1f61ebacadce944ed1e301}{value\+\_\+type}} \&}]{val}{, }\item[{Func}]{func}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}}]{b\+Allow\+Insert}{ = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a41f9c5fb8b08eb5dc3edce4dcb37fee7}{true}}}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Updates the item 

The operation performs inserting or changing data with lock-\/free manner.

If the item {\ttfamily val} not found in the list, then {\ttfamily val} is inserted into the list iff {\ttfamily b\+Allow\+Insert} is {\ttfamily true}. Otherwise, the functor {\ttfamily func} is called with item found. The functor signature is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{operator()}}(\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{bNew}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{item}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{val}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 with arguments\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily b\+New} -\/ {\ttfamily true} if the item has been inserted, {\ttfamily false} otherwise
\item {\ttfamily item} -\/ item of the list
\item {\ttfamily val} -\/ argument {\ttfamily val} passed into the {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a48eac62d210964a761201eebcbded9a6}{update()}} function If new item has been inserted (i.\+e. {\ttfamily b\+New} is {\ttfamily true}) then {\ttfamily item} and {\ttfamily val} arguments refer to the same thing.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor may change non-\/key fields of the {\ttfamily item}. While the functor {\ttfamily f} is working the item {\ttfamily item} is locked, so {\ttfamily func} has exclusive access to the item.

Returns {\ttfamily  std\+::pair$<$bool, bool$>$ } where {\ttfamily first} is {\ttfamily true} if operation is successful, {\ttfamily second} is {\ttfamily true} if new item has been added or {\ttfamily false} if the item with {\ttfamily key} already is in the list.

The function makes RCU lock internally. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a48eac62d210964a761201eebcbded9a6}\index{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!update@{update}}
\index{update@{update}!cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::LazyList$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{update()}{update()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a48eac62d210964a761201eebcbded9a6} 
template$<$typename RCU, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, class Traits$>$ \\
template$<$typename Func$>$ \\
std\+::pair$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Lazy\+List}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_af8e0fb00fa1f61ebacadce944ed1e301}{value\+\_\+type}} \&}]{val}{, }\item[{Func}]{func}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}}]{b\+Allow\+Insert}{ = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a41f9c5fb8b08eb5dc3edce4dcb37fee7}{true}}}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Updates the item 

The operation performs inserting or changing data with lock-\/free manner.

If the item {\ttfamily val} not found in the list, then {\ttfamily val} is inserted into the list iff {\ttfamily b\+Allow\+Insert} is {\ttfamily true}. Otherwise, the functor {\ttfamily func} is called with item found. The functor signature is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{operator()}}(\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{bNew}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{item}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list}{val}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 with arguments\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily b\+New} -\/ {\ttfamily true} if the item has been inserted, {\ttfamily false} otherwise
\item {\ttfamily item} -\/ item of the list
\item {\ttfamily val} -\/ argument {\ttfamily val} passed into the {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a48eac62d210964a761201eebcbded9a6}{update()}} function If new item has been inserted (i.\+e. {\ttfamily b\+New} is {\ttfamily true}) then {\ttfamily item} and {\ttfamily val} arguments refer to the same thing.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor may change non-\/key fields of the {\ttfamily item}. While the functor {\ttfamily f} is calling the item {\ttfamily item} is locked.

Returns {\ttfamily  std\+::pair$<$bool, bool$>$ } where {\ttfamily first} is {\ttfamily true} if operation is successful, {\ttfamily second} is {\ttfamily true} if new item has been added or {\ttfamily false} if the item with {\ttfamily key} already is in the list.

The function makes RCU lock internally.
